sprang mo lab sgron nga/ ale
/bzang yang bzang la ngan yang ngan/ US
/bzang nas grub thob kyi brgyud pa 'dzin/
/ngan nas 'khor du mdzo sprang bsten/
/dam chos mnyam pa ris med kyi gdams pa bdog/

'o na 'dir dpa' nas sdod dam 'dar nas sdod zer bar/ sa phyogs
med kyi sprang mo lab sgron nga/

/dpa' nas gnyan sa phyogs med 'grims/

l'dar nas 'khor ba'i nyes amigs 'jigs/

/pha yul dang 'grogs te chos shig by ed snyam yang/
/pha yul ni bdud kyi btson rar 'dug/
/sems nyid kyi rta la rgyug sa med/
sprang mos de'i phyir pha yul spangs pa lags/
/sprang mo'i yul skal du rgyal khams phyogs med byung/
Iyul la phyogs ris med pas sprang mozhe blo bde/
/pha khu dang 'groge nas 1ha chos byed bgam yang/
/pha khu'i nga royal ri rab bas kyang mtho/
/sems bskyed kyi nyi ma 'char dus med/
/sprang mos de'i phyir pha khu spangs pa lags/
sprang mo'i gnyen skal du drin can bla ma byung/
aka' spyad pha phogs su byed pa sprang mo zhe blo bde/
Ignyen ma sru dang 'grogs nas lha chos by ed snyam yang/
/ma sru ni dug gi phor pa 'dra/
/gdams ngag gi bdud rtsi lug sa med/
/sprang mos de'i phyir ma sru spangs pa lags/
/sprang mo'i ma sru ra (f. 29r) sems pa bzang po byung/
/gdams ngag gcig gi grol bas sprang mo zhe blo bde/
Igtan grogs dang 'grogs nas lha chos byed bsam yang/
/grogs ngan de byur gyi gnya' shing du 'dug/
/rang gang 'dod du 'gro dbang med pas na/
/ sprang mo'i de'i phyir gtan grogs spangs pa lags/
sprang mos grogs skal du rang byung ye shes byung/
/grogs 'du 'bral med pas sprang mo che blo bde/
/rang skyes bu phrug dang 'grogs nas lha chos by ed bsam yang/
/bu phrug mams 'khor ba'i zhags thag tu 'dug/
/'khor ba nas thon thabs med pas na/
/ sprang mos de'i phyir bu phrug spangs pa lags/
/sprang mo'i bu skal du rig pa'i khye'u chung byung/
/bou skye 'chi med pas sprang mo che blo bde/
/nor zang zing dang 'grogs nas lha chos byed bsam yang/
/nor bsags srus ni dmyal ba'i bud shing rgyu/
/sprang mos de'i phyir bsags srung spangs pa lags/
/sprang mo'i nor skal du sens kyi gter kha 'byed/
/nor zad pa med pas sprang mozhe blo bde/ /zhes gsungs pas/
mkhan po 'khor dang bcas pa dad pa lhag par skyes nas/ phyag gyang
gyel ba ltar (f. 29v) btsal/ khyed grub thob chen mo gcig 'dug/
bdag cag mams kyi skur ba btab pa bzod par bzhes par gsol/ sku
gcer bu lai 'dra cung mi 'thad/ btsun chas zhig 'bul bas rab tu

RGYAL-SRAS PADMA-'JIGS-BRAL (1730-1761+)
/rgyal sras padma 'jigs bral gyi rnam par thar pa bkod pa
rgyal sras nyid kyi zhal gsung gi mnam thar las mdor bsdus zur
tsam bkod na yab rje'phrin las rnam rgyal gyi mam thar du/
kun mkhyen chos dbang bras ljongs su bzhugs skabs yab rjer gong

pa ni dngos 'brel/ kun mkhyen chos dbang slar zhing 'di'i giul
bya skyong ba'i slad du mchog gi sprul par mngon sum mtshan mas
grub pa/ rgyal sras padma 'jigs bral rang khams su sku bltams
pa'i tshul/ yab gter ston g.ya! chal sngon po'i sku rigs rig

gzhung nor rgyas klu lding pa'i bu mo karma chos sgron zhes/
dam pa'i gsang lung las/
mon mo'i sprul pa karma'i ming/

zhugs/
sngar gong ma'i 'phrod lam la dgongs te g.yang chos dbu
mdzad mkha' dbyings par bu "dzin bskos te/bres dgon nas gsang

dus gya ring shar ba'i zhing sa'i steng gzim gur phub nas bzhugs/

thag yab rje mchog nas/ bkra shis rtags brgyad dar gyis g.yogs
shing/ ljags steng dri bzang gi a bri ba sogs byis bcos rnans
yongs su rdzogs pa ndzad de/ mtshan SIDDHI DPAL MGON du 'dogs
pa gnang/ de'i nyin gangs bab chad nam mkha' dwangs zhing sprin
'ja' mang pos khyab pa sogs rtags bzang ba dang/ tshes bcu'i

de nas yum sras nyung 'dus zhabs zhu bcas gsang stabs kyis

SKU-YE RJE 'PHRIN-LAS-RNAM-RGYAL ('Gyur-ned-...)
/bdag gi gsum ldan rtsa ba'i bla ma sku ye te 'phrin las
man rgyal gyi sku'i rus ni sngar bod sa li'i ljongs kyi dus
su rgya gar du li sa'i rigs las gyerssgom pa ting ezin la
mnga' brnyes pa zhig stel de la dpal idan lha mo nched gsuma
gyi khyed rang gi gdul bya bod kyi yul gas theg pa bya ba
zhig na yod pas/ nged kyi gdan 'dren zer dred mo zhig gi rgyab
la gdan drangs nas skad cig de nyid la mkhar rta bsan rtse'i
guas theg pa'i phug pa der bskyal der bzhugs dgos byung yang
yo byad sogs 'phrin las dpal lha mo rang gi bsgrubs/ chos dang
rigs brgyud spel dgos pa'i lung bstan la brten/ da lta SBREG

'dug kyang mig mthong na gyur/
